            (function() {
              function trackAndRedirect(action, url, event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                if (typeof window.melidata === 'function') {
                  try {
                    window.melidata('send', 'event', {
                      path: '/suspicious_traffic',
                      event_data: { action: action }
                    });
                  } catch {
                  }
                }

                setTimeout(function() {
                  window.location.href = url;
                }, 10);
              }
              
              if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initTracking);
              } else {
                initTracking();
              }
              
              function initTracking() {
                // Desktop buttons
                var newUserBtn = document.querySelector('.new-user-button');
                var oldUserBtn = document.querySelector('.old-user-button');
                
                if (newUserBtn) {
                  newUserBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    trackAndRedirect('new_user', this.href, e);
                  });
                }
                
                if (oldUserBtn) {
                  oldUserBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    trackAndRedirect('old_user', this.href, e);
                  });
                }
                
                // Mobile buttons
                var downloadBtn = document.querySelector('.download-app-button-mobile');
                if (downloadBtn) {
                  var isAndroid = downloadBtn.href.includes('play.google.com');
                  var action = isAndroid ? 'download_android_app' : 'download_ios_app';
                  
                  downloadBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    trackAndRedirect(action, this.href, e);
                  });
                }
              }
            })();
